FROM (
    SELECT TOP(2) [c].[id], [c].[created_at], [c].[name], [c].[updated_at]
    FROM [Category] AS [c]
    WHERE UPPER([c].[name]) = @__ToUpper_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c0].[id], [c0].[category_id], [c0].[created_at], [c0].[job_advertisement_id], [c0].[updated_at], [j].[id] AS [id0], [j].[benefit], [j].[company], [j].[created_at] AS [created_at0], [j].[date_limit], [j].[description], [j].[email], [j].[is_active], [j].[link], [j].[max_payrange], [j].[min_payrange], [j].[modality], [j].[monthly_hours], [j].[phone_number], [j].[requerements], [j].[title], [j].[updated_at] AS [updated_at0], [j].[user_id], [a].[id] AS [id1], [a].[city], [a].[country], [a].[created_at] AS [created_at1], [a].[district], [a].[job_advertisement_id] AS [job_advertisement_id0], [a].[state], [a].[street], [a].[updated_at] AS [updated_at1]
    FROM [CategoryJob] AS [c0]
    INNER JOIN [JobAdvertisement] AS [j] ON [c0].[job_advertisement_id] = [j].[id]
    LEFT JOIN [Address] AS [a] ON [j].[id] = [a].[job_advertisement_id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[id] = [t0].[category_id]
ORDER BY [t].[id], [t0].[id], [t0].[id0]
